     <script type="text/javascript">
      //!INLINE JS TO BE MOVED
$(function(){
var browseTrigger = $('#browse-trigger'),
browseMenu = $('#browse-menu'),
overflowTrigger = $('.phoneOverflow'),
overflowMenu = $('#overflow-menu'),
menuList = $('.browseCategory', browseMenu);
subMenuList = $('.subCategory', browseMenu)
browseTrigger.on("click", function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
if (browseMenu.hasClass("open")) {
browseMenu.removeClass("open")
browseTrigger.removeClass("open");
} else {
//close overflow
overflowTrigger.removeClass("open");
overflowMenu.removeClass("open");
browseMenu.addClass("open");
browseTrigger.addClass("open");
}
});
browseMenu.on("mouseenter", function(e) {
browseMenu.on("mouseleave", function(e) {
browseMenu.removeClass("open");
browseTrigger.removeClass("open");
});
});
// if (mlbSettings.device === "phone") {
$('.overflow-trigger').on("click", function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
if (overflowMenu.hasClass("open")) {
overflowMenu.removeClass("open")
overflowTrigger.removeClass("open");
} else {
//close browse menu if open
browseMenu.removeClass("open");
browseTrigger.removeClass("open");
overflowMenu.addClass("open");
overflowTrigger.addClass("open");
}
});
// }
$('.expandable', menuList).click(function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
var subCatId = $(this).data("id"),
allSubMenus = $(subMenuList).find("ul"),
subMenuWanted = $(subMenuList).find("ul[id="+ subCatId +"]"),
subMenuTitle = subMenuWanted.attr("data-catHeadline");
subMenuList.find("div.catHeadline").html(subMenuTitle);
allSubMenus.hide();
subMenuWanted.show();
menuList.animate({
left: parseInt(menuList.css('left'),10) == 0 ?
1500 : 0
});
subMenuList.animate({
left: parseInt(subMenuList.css('left'),10) == 0 ?
1500 : 0
});
});
$('.back', subMenuList).click(function() {
menuList.animate({
left: subMenuList.css("left")
});
var menuListPos = parseInt(menuList.css("left"));
subMenuList.animate({
left: menuListPos *= -1 //inverse to send menu back to the right
});
});
$('input.deletable').wrap('&lt;span class="deleteicon" /&gt;').after($('&lt;span class="icon"/&gt;').click(function() {
$(this).prev('input').val("").focus();
$('.icon', '.deleteicon').hide();
}));
if ($("input.deletable").val() !== "Search") {
$('.icon', '.deleteicon').show();
}
$("input.deletable").on({
keyup: function() {
if ($(this).val() !== "") {
$('.icon', '.deleteicon').show();
} else {
$('.icon', '.deleteicon').hide();
}
}
});
});
     </script>
